                   <div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}'>
                    <p>
                     A video preview of FALLING: NEW VISIONS DIRECTORS&#039; FESTIVAL, which opens tonight — through Sunday!
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     The evening features Oscar Wilde&#039;s &quot;Salome,&quot; directed by
                     <span class="profileLink">
                      Simon Evans
                     </span>
                     , and Sam Shepard&#039;s &quot;Icarus&#039;s Mother,&quot; directed by
                     <a class="profileLink" href="https://www.facebook.com/karina.fox.31">
                      Karina Fox
                     </a>
                     . Video produced by
                     <a class="profileLink" href="https://www.facebook.com/anne.kitz">
                      Anne Kitz
                     </a>
                     .
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Tickets:

                    <div id="id_583f4899aa1c08294094961" class="text_exposed_root">
                     <p>
                      Students, Alumni, Fans, and Friends:
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      FEEL THE
                      <a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/mulementum?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=10154874214706037" data-ft='{"tn":"*N","type":104}'>
                       <span class="_5afx">

                         #
                        </span>
                        <span class="_58cm">
                         MULEMENTUM
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </a>
                      TODAY! Join the Muhlenberg Community in showing your support for Berg! Today is all about participation — every gift is GREAT, no matter what size!
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      If you want to earmark your gift for Theatre &amp; Dance, just say so in the comment field or let the folks at the tables in Seegers and Life Sports Center know your preference. If you DO earmark your contribution, we&#039;ll use it to bring great guest artists to campus, create sp
                      <span class="text_exposed_hide">
                       ...
                      </span>
                      <span class="text_exposed_show">
                       ectacular programs, and do educational outreach through our Summer Imagination Workshops!
                      </span>
                     </p>

                              Muhlenberg raises “Pirates of Penzance” to next level
                             </a>
                            </div>
                            <div class="_6m7 _3bt9">
                             Gilbert and Sullivan is always enjoyable, but Muhlenberg College has taken its production of the comic operetta &quot;Pirates of Penzance,&quot; to the next level.
                            </div>
                            <div class="_59tj _2iau">

                              Theater: &#039;Pirates of Penzance&#039; with a twist at Muhlenberg College
                             </a>

                            <div class="_6m7 _3bt9">
                             A classic Gilbert and Sullivan comic operetta gets a new twist in Muhlenberg College&#039;s production of &quot;Pirates of Penzance,&quot; running Friday through Nov. 6.
                            </div>
